If you would like to view the full original source code of Speed (latest version) then you will have to play this game. The full source is uploaded somewhere on the internet as a zip file. Below there are a list of 20000 strings, one of which is the code for a url shortening url. You have to figure out which url shortener I used, then find the code in the list below. The code is definitely in the list and it is definitely uploaded somewhere. Good luck!
